 co / p26xyqac7d The Supreme Court today dismissed the petition filed against Ranbaxy Laboratories Ltd for making and selling substandard medicines for lack of evidence
 is nirnay ke baavjood nyaayamurti eke patnayak or nyaayamurti ranjan gogoi kii peeth ne yachikakarta adhivaktaa emel sharma se kaha ki yadi unhen kuch sakshya mil jaaen to ve phir se yachika daayar kar sakate hai
 The petition alleged that the company produces and sells substandard drugs
 peeth ne kaha ki vah america adaalat dwaara company ke khilaaf die gaye faisle ke aadhaar par is yachika par faisla nahin de sakati
 The bench said, "your argument is based on the American court process
" yah hamaare kshetradhikaar main nahin aata
 Show us such evidence that these things are happening in India and this is affecting people's right to live
 ranbaxy ke khilaaf koi thos sakshya kahaan hai? The court said, no evidence has been produced in this regard to prove that the drugs manufactured in any of Ranbaxy's factories are substandard, adulterated, counterfeit and the drugs are banned
 aise kisi pramaan ke abhaav main is yachika par sunwaayee nahin kii ja sakati he
 The comments sharma ne apni yachika main daleel di thi america khaadya evam dawa prashasan (uasapadie) ne company par milavati dawaaen banane or bikri ke sambandh main 50 karod dollar kaa jurmaana lagaaya he
 In this, the company also demanded closure of the factories at Ponta Sahib in Himachal Pradesh and Dewas in Madhya Pradesh
 unhone aarope lagaaya ki ranbaxy ne america main milavati dawaaon kii aapurti kaa dosha sweekaar kiya or company par baari-bharkam jurmaana lagaaya gaya
 Despite this, the central government in India did not take any initiative to restrict the medicines made by the company
 sharma ne is maamle main america jaanch ke parinaam aane ke baad bhi company ko bharat main dawa bechney kii anumati dene ke khilaaf bhartiya dawa niamak kendriya dawa maanak niyantran sanghathan (sidissio) ke khilaaf karrwai kiye jane kii bhi maang kii thi
 Despite this decision, a bench of Justice AK Patnaik and Justice Ranjan Gogoi told the petitioner advocate ML Sharma that if they get some evidence, they can file the petition again
 yachika main aarope lagaaya gaya tha ki company ghatiya dawaaon kaa utpaadan or bikri karti he
 The bench said that it cannot pass judgment on this petition based on the judgment given by the US court against the company
 peeth ne kaha, aapaki daleel america kii adalati prakriya par aadhaarit he
 It does not come under our jurisdiction
 hamen aise sakshya dikhaaen ki bharat main ye chijen ho rahi hai or isse logon ke jeene kaa adhikaar prabhavit ho rahaa he
 Where is the hard evidence against Ranbaxy? nyaayalay ne kaha, is sambandh main koi pramaan prastut nahin kiya gaya he, jisase yah siddh ho sake ki ranbaxy ke kisi bhi kaarkaane main vinirmit kii gai dawaaen ghatiya, milavati, nakli he or in davaavon par kanoon pabandi he
 In the absence of any such evidence, this petition cannot be heard
 tippaniyan Sharma had argued in his petition that the US Food and Drug Administration (USFDA) has fined the company $ 500 million in connection with the manufacture and sale of adulterated drugs
 isamen company kii himachal pradesh ke ponta sahib or madhyapradesh ke devas ke kaarkaanon ko band karaane kii bhi maang kii gai thi
 He alleged that Ranbaxy admitted to supplying adulterated drugs to the US and was fined heavily
 iske baavjood bharat main centre sarkaar ne company dwaara banaai gai dawaaon ko pratibandhit karne ke liye koi pahal nahin kii
 Sharma also demanded action against the Indian drug regulator Central Drug Standards Control Organization (CDSCO) against allowing the company to sell the drug in India, even after the results of the US investigation into the case

 bharat ne ek baar phir se china kii ‘belt and road inishiative’ (biarai) ko lekar hone vaali baithak kaa bahishkaar karne ke sanket die hai
 China claims that representatives of more than 100 countries are going to attend the second meeting of the 'belt and Road Initiative'
 ek varisht chini adhikari ne shanivaar ko bataaya ki is baithak main kareeb 40 deshon ke sarkaar ke netaa bhi hissaa lenge
 Earlier, China held its first BRI meeting in 2017, which India boycotted
 biarai china ke raashtrapati shi jinping kii sabase pasandida pariyojna he
 The aim of this project is to develop infrastructural projects and increase China's dominance with Chinese investment worldwide
 bharat ne pehali biarai baithak kaa bahishkaar karne ke baad ab duusari baithak kaa bahishkaar karne kaa man bana liya he
 India is opposed to China's BRI because the china-pakistan Economic Corridor passes through Pakistan-occupied Kashmir (pok)
 bharat isko apni samprabhutaa kaa ulanghan bataata he
 India says pok is part of India and is illegally occupied by Pakistan
 aise main bharat kii ijaajat ke bina china pioke se aarthik galiyara nahin bana saktaa he
 If China passes the china-pakistan Economic Corridor through pok, it is a violation of India's sovereignty
 haal hi main china main bharat ke rajdoot vikram misari ne china ke sarkari akhbaar global times ko die ek saakshaatkaar main duusari biarai baithak kaa bhi bahishkaar karne kii baat kahi thi
 At the same time, China's State Counselor Yang Jiechi said in an interview to state-run news agency Xinhua that representatives of more than 100 countries, including leaders of governments of 40 countries, will participate in the second meeting of the BRI
 kya he BRI project?biarai china ke raashtrapati shi jinping kaa mahatvakankshi project he
 China has brought the BRI project to overcome the economic downturn, tackle unemployment and revive the economy
 iske tahat china ne asia, europe or africa ko sadak maarg, railmarg, gas pipe line or bandargah se jodne ke liye silk road iconomic belt or meritime silk road pariyojna shuru kii he
 There are plans to build six corridors under the BRI, out of which work is going on on several corridors
 isamen pakistan adhikrut kashmir (pioke) se guzarane vaala china-pakistan aarthik galiyara bhi shaamil he
 Many countries of the world including India have already expressed concern, many countries including India and America have expressed concern about the BRI of China

 is match main super kings kamjor dikh rahi daire davills ke khilaaf badi jeet ke iraade ke saath maidan main utregi
